# Partie I

# ğŸš€ Installer Docker sur votre Machine Azure

### ğŸ—ï¸ Set up Docker's apt repository.

````
Add Docker's official GPG key:
sudo apt-get update
sudo apt-get install ca-certificates curl
sudo install -m 0755 -d /etc/apt/keyrings
sudo curl -fsSL https://download.docker.com/linux/ubuntu/gpg -o /etc/apt/keyrings/docker.asc
sudo chmod a+r /etc/apt/keyrings/docker.asc

# Add the repository to Apt sources:
echo \
  "deb [arch=$(dpkg --print-architecture) signed-by=/etc/apt/keyrings/docker.asc] https://download.docker.com/linux/ubuntu \
  $(. /etc/os-release && echo "${UBUNTU_CODENAME:-$VERSION_CODENAME}") stable" | \
  sudo tee /etc/apt/sources.list.d/docker.list > /dev/null
sudo apt-get update
````

### ğŸ› ï¸ Install the Docker packages.
````
sudo apt-get install docker-ce docker-ce-cli containerd.io docker-buildx-plugin docker-compose-plugin
````

### âœ… VÃ©rification que Docker soit bien installÃ©

````
sudo docker run hello-world
````

# Partie II

# ğŸš€ DÃ©ploiement d'un Serveur Apache dans un Conteneur Docker

## ğŸ“Œ PrÃ©paration de l'environnement

### ğŸ“ CrÃ©ation du rÃ©pertoire de travail
 
````
azureuser@TP:~$ sudo mkdir image_docker_tp
azureuser@TP:~$ cd image_docker_tp
````

# ğŸ—ï¸ CrÃ©ation de l'Image Docker

### ğŸ“œ RÃ©daction du Dockerfile
````
azureuser@TP:~/image_docker_tp$ sudo nano Dockerfile
````

**Contenu du `Dockerfile`**
````
FROM debian:latest

RUN apt update -y && apt install -y apache2

COPY apache2.conf /etc/apache2/apache2.conf

COPY index.html /var/www/html/index.html

EXPOSE 80

CMD [ "apache2", "-DFOREGROUND" ]

````

# ğŸ”§ Configuration d'Apache2

### ğŸ“œ RÃ©daction du fichier `apache2.conf`
````
azureuser@TP:~/image_docker_tp$ sudo nano apache2.conf
````

**Contenu de `apache2.conf`**
````
ServerName 4.221.118.11

Listen 80

LoadModule mpm_event_module "/usr/lib/apache2/modules/mod_mpm_event.so"
LoadModule dir_module "/usr/lib/apache2/modules/mod_dir.so"
LoadModule authz_core_module "/usr/lib/apache2/modules/mod_authz_core.so"

DirectoryIndex index.html

DocumentRoot "/var/www/html/"

ErrorLog "/var/log/apache2/error.log"
LogLevel warn
````

# ğŸŒ CrÃ©ation d'une Page Web PersonnalisÃ©e

### ğŸ“œ RÃ©daction du fichier `index.html`

````
azureuser@TP:~/image_docker_tp$ sudo nano index.html
````

**Contenu de `index.html`**
````
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="fr">
<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8">
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">
    <title>Serveur Apache Docker</title>
</head>
<body>
    <h1>Bienvenue sur mon serveur Apache dans un conteneur Docker !</h1>
    <p>Mon serveur tourne sur Debian et utilise Apache2.</p>
</body>
</html>
````

### ğŸ—ï¸ Construction de l'Image Docker
````
docker build . -t image_docker_tp   

````

### ğŸ” VÃ©rification de l'Image Docker

````
azureuser@TP:~/image_docker_tp$ docker images
REPOSITORY        TAG       IMAGE ID       CREATED              SIZE
image_docker_tp   latest    aa6b0502a699   About a minute ago   253MB
nginx             latest    b52e0b094bc0   5 weeks ago          192MB
hello-world       latest    74cc54e27dc4   7 weeks ago          10.1kB
````

### ğŸš€ Lancement du Conteneur
````
azureuser@TP:~/image_docker_tp$ docker run -p 8080:80 image_docker_tp
````

### ğŸ› ï¸ VÃ©rification avec``curl``

# Partie III

## ğŸ“Œ DÃ©ploiement de WikiJS avec Docker

**âœ… CrÃ©ation du dossier et du fichier docker-compose.yml**
````
azureuser@TP:~$ mkdir wikijs && cd wikijs
azureuser@TP:~$ sudo nano docker-compose.yml
````

**fichier `docker-compose.yml`**
````
version: "3.8"

services:
  db:
    image: postgres:13
    restart: always
    environment:
      POSTGRES_DB: wikijs
      POSTGRES_USER: wikijs
      POSTGRES_PASSWORD: mysecretpassword
    volumes:
      - db-data:/var/lib/postgresql/data

  wikijs:
    image: requarks/wiki:latest
    restart: always
    depends_on:
      - db
    ports:
      - "80:3000"
    environment:
      DB_TYPE: postgres
      DB_HOST: db
      DB_PORT: 5432
      DB_USER: wikijs
      DB_PASS: mysecretpassword
      DB_NAME: wikijs

volumes:
  db-data:

````

### âœ… Lancement de WikiJS
````
azureuser@TP:~/wikijs$ docker-compose up -d
````

**ajout de l'utilisateur au group `Docker`**
````
sudo usermod -aG docker $USER
````
